msg:The room is spacious, with high ceilings, thick carpets, good support and softness of the bed, and the bed is big enough, which are all plus points.
Here are the bad points. There are yellow marks on the outer shell of the hand cream in the bathroom. I don't know what it is, so I didn't dare to look at it. Anyway, just use your own.
The breakfast variety is very rich, but the ingredients are poor. There are broken bones in the meatballs, which almost broke my teeth. It looks like a German grilled sausage mixed with celery, but it's pure starch. The stir-fry area is bean sprouts, cabbage, and rapeseed, whatever is the cheapest. Flower rolls, buns, and steamed dumplings are all frozen products. The hotel price is 68 per person, and the price of the Ctrip order seems to be only 50 yuan for two people. It's cheap and it's not delicious.
Many children ran around and coughed wildly at the food in the public dining area. There were also guests who walked out while drinking drinks after dinner, and put the empty drink cups on the table where we just started eating, which was extremely rude. Of course, this is a problem of guest quality, but it would be better if the hotel could advise them.
